本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Marine Electrical and Electronic Engineering Major
[2024级适用]
环境工程（082502）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
环境工程专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Environmental Engineering Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
大连海事大学环境工程专业创建于1995年，是学校重点建设的品牌专业之一。2008年入选辽宁省高等学校示范性专业。2020年被认定为辽宁省一流本科专业。目前每年招生规模为两个自然班，共约60人。专业现有专职教师45人，其中博士生导师9人、教授8人、副教授27人、讲师10人，42人具有博士学位。另有专职实验教师4人，其中博士1人。
本专业的培养方案贯彻宽口径、厚基础的办学宗旨，坚持立足港航、面向全国的办学特色。主要专业方向有环境污染控制工程和环境评价与管理。本专业拥有1个省级重点实验室和1个辽宁省船舶节能环保工程技术研究中心，具有环境科学与工程学科博士学位授予点、环境科学与工程一级学科硕士学位授予点、环境工程学科专业硕士学位授予点，这为有志于进一步深造的同学提供了广阔的平台及发展空间。
Established in 1995, the Environmental Engineering major is one of the key major of Dalian Maritime University. In 2008, the major was selected by Liaoning Province authorities as a provincial demonstrative program of higher learning. In 2020, the major was approved by Liaoning Province authorities as a provincial first-rate major. At present, the major enrolls about 60 students for two natural classes each year. There are 42 specialized teachers for the major, including 17 doctoral degree supervisors, 9 professors, 25 associate professors, and 8 lecturers; 41 of which are Ph.D. graduates. In addition, there are 4 specialized experiment instructors, one of which holds a doctoral degree.
The professional training program to implement the school-running aim of wide and strong basic knowledge, adheres to our own feature, facing the whole country's school-running characteristics. The main direction of this major is engineering of environmental pollution control, environmental assessment and management. With the establishment of a provincial key laboratory and the Liaoning Research Center of Energy Saving and Environmental Protection Engineering Technology for Ships, as well as a doctoral degree program in Environmental Science and Engineering, a master’s degree program in Environmental Science and Engineering, and a professional master's degree program in Environmental Engineering, the Environmental Engineering major offered by Dalian Maritime University provides a broad platform and development space for those wishing to further their studies.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
针对海洋和港航为主区域生态建设和环境保护，本专业培养具备良好的人文素养、职业道德和社会责任感，系统掌握化学和环境工程的基础理论、专业知识和实验研究方法，具有环境污染防治工程设计及运营管理能力、开展环境评价规划和环境质量监测的能力，以及环境工程方向的新理论、新工艺和新设备的研究和开发能力，具有一定创新意识和较强工程实践能力，良好的人际交往及团队合作能力，能够综合运用环境工程及相关学科理论和专业知识，在相关行业或部门从事环境工程设计、施工与运营管理、评价规划、技术咨询、教育培训、研究开发等工作的应用型高级专业人才。
预期学生在毕业五年后，经过自身学习和工作锻炼，能够达到下列职业和专业能力：
具有跨文化协同和团队协调能力；
在环境保护领域具有系统思维、可持续发展理念和多学科知识交叉融合与迁移能力；
在环境工程领域具备创新性解决不确定环境下复杂工程项目能力；
具有工程伦理道德责任，尊重社会价值；
具备组织及协作领导能力，具备批判和反思能力；
具备终生学习和专业发展能力
In response to ecological construction and environmental protection in areas primarily focused on oceans, ports, and shipping, this major aims to cultivate application-oriented technical talents with good humanistic qualities, professional ethics and social responsibility who are engaged in environmental engineering design, construction and operation management, evaluation and planning, technical consultation, education and training, and research and development in related industries or departments. They should master basic theories, professional knowledge and experimental research methods of chemical and environmental engineering systematically; have the ability to design, operate and manage environmental pollution prevention and control projects, carry out environmental evaluation planning and environmental quality monitoring, research and develop new theories, processes and equipment in the direction of environmental engineering, have a certain consciousness of innovation and strong engineering practice ability; have good interpersonal and teamwork skills, and be able to comprehensively apply environmental engineering and related theories as well as professional knowledge.
It is expected that students, after five years of graduation, will be able to achieve the following professional abilities through their own learning and work training:
(1) Cross-cultural collaboration and team coordination skills;
(2) Systematic thinking, sustainable development concepts, and interdisciplinary knowledge in the field of environmental protection;
(3) The ability to creatively solve complex engineering projects in uncertain environments in the field of environmental engineering;
(4) Engineering ethics moral responsibility and respect social values;
(5) Organizational and collaborative leadership skills, as well as critical and reflective abilities;
(6) Lifelong learning and professional development abilities.
三、毕业要求
III．Graduation Requirements
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
环境工程原理、水污染控制工程、大气污染控制工程、固体废物处理与处置、国际海洋污染防治法规、船舶与港口污染防治技术、非热放电环境污染治理技术。
Environmental Engineering Principle, Water Pollution Control Engineering, Air Pollution Control Engineering, Treatment and Disposal of Solid Waste, Marine Pollution Control Laws, Ship And Port Pollution Prevention Technology, Environmental Remediation Using Non-thermal Plasma.

后    记
培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，培养计划原则上每4年修订一次，在特殊情况下可提前或推迟进行修订，我校培养计划上一次全面修订于2021年进行。为满足教育教学改革的需要，本年度培养计划在2023年修订版的基础上进行了再次修订。
本年度培养计划在多次校对、反复审核的过程当中，得到了各教学单位领导、教务、以及老师的大力支持和帮助。在此，对在培养计划修订过程中给予支持和帮助的各位，表示衷心的感谢。
培养计划的制定是一项繁琐的系统工作，难免会有疏漏，不足之处还望批评指正。培养计划的修订是以专业发展和知识更新为需求导向的，在执行过程中会进行细微调整。在此过程中，若产生分歧，应以教务系统为准。

本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Marine Science Major
[2024级适用]
海洋科学（070701）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
海洋科学专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Marine Science Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
海洋科学专业培养具备海洋科学的基本理论、基础知识和基本技能，能在海洋科学及相关领域从事科研、教学、管理及技术工作的专门人才。本专业学生具有坚实的数学、化学、物理学及海洋科学方面的基本理论和基础知识，受到海洋科学研究方面的基本训练，掌握海洋科学调查方法和实验技能，具备从事海洋调查和海洋科学研究的基本能力。
The Marine Science Major is set up to cultivate professional students with the basic theory, knowledge and skill in marine science, which can work in the related field of marine science for research, education, management and planning. The graduated students have solid basic theory and knowledge of math, physics and marine science, have been well trained for marine science research, master basic methods and experimental skills for ocean survey and observation, and thus have ability for ocean survey and marine science research.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业主要培养具备海洋科学领域所需的基础理论和专业知识，掌握海洋污染监测、航运污染治理与生态修复、海洋环境管理与规划等方面的专业知识和技能，服务海洋强国战略和交通强国战略建设的高素质专业人才。本专业学生毕业后可以在政府海洋管理部门、海洋规划部门、海洋环境保护部门及其它相关的设计和科研单位从事海洋规划、管理、技术开发、教育和研究等方面工作。
This major aim to cultivate students with the basic theory and special knowledge in marine science, and essential skills in Marine pollution monitoring, Vessel-source pollution control and ecological restoration, Marine environment management and planning. The graduates are expected to engage in planning, management, education and research works for governmental departments, planning departments, marine economic administrations, marine environmental protection departments, designing institutes, industrial and mining enterprises, researching institutes, universities, etc., as the integrated developed technical talents in marine engineering and environmental administration.
三、毕业要求
III．Graduation Requirements
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
化学海洋学、物理海洋学、海洋生物学、海洋地质学
Chemical Oceanography, Physical Oceanography, Marine Biology, Marine Geology

后    记
培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，培养计划原则上每4年修订一次，在特殊情况下可提前或推迟进行修订，我校培养计划上一次全面修订于2021年进行。为满足教育教学改革的需要，本年度培养计划在2023年修订版的基础上进行了再次修订。
本年度培养计划在多次校对、反复审核的过程当中，得到了各教学单位领导、教务、以及老师的大力支持和帮助。在此，对在培养计划修订过程中给予支持和帮助的各位，表示衷心的感谢。
培养计划的制定是一项繁琐的系统工作，难免会有疏漏，不足之处还望批评指正。培养计划的修订是以专业发展和知识更新为需求导向的，在执行过程中会进行细微调整。在此过程中，若产生分歧，应以教务系统为准。

海洋资源与环境（070703T）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
海洋资源与环境专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Marine Resources and Environment Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
海洋资源与环境专业培养具有坚实的数理化和生物学的基本理论和基本知识，具有环境化学检测、环境毒理学和现代生物学分析技术；掌握海洋生态环境监测与评估、海洋生物技术与资源开发等基本技能；在德、智、体、美全面发展的高级技术人才。主要专业基础课包括：有机化学及实验、环境化学、基础生态学、海洋生物学及实验、生物化学及实验、分子生物学、细胞生物学及实验、遗传学、微生物学及实验、人体及动物生理学及实验、环境毒理学、生物信息学、生物统计建模、基因工程、环境生物修复技术、微流控生物分析技术基础、海洋管理概论、海洋环境评价等。
The undergraduate program for the major of Marine Resources and Environment aims to cultivate students with the basic theory and knowledge in Mathematics, Physics, Chemistry and Biology Science, essential techniques in environmental chemistry monitoring, environmental toxicology and modern biological analysis, as well as basic skills in marine environmental monitoring, marine biotechnology and resource development. The main degree courses included: Organic Chemistry and Experiments, Environmental Chemistry, Basic Ecology, Marine Biology and Experiments, Biochemistry and Experiments, Molecular biology, Cell biology and Experiments, Genetics, Microbiology and Experiment, Human and Animal Physiology  and Experiments, Environmental Toxicology, Bioinformatics, Biostatistics Modeling, Genetic Engineering, Environmental Biology    Repair Technology, Fundamentals of Micro-fluidic analysis Technology, Introduction to Marine Management and Marine environmental assessment, etc.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
海洋资源与环境专业在海洋生物技术与资源开发、环境污染监测与生态修复、环境风险评估三个方向进行特色建设。重点培养学生具有坚实的数理化和生物学的基本理论和基本知识，具有从事海洋生物资源与环境调查评价、海洋生物资源增殖与养护、海洋生物资源可持续利用等技术研发与管理能力，了解海洋生物资源与环境的国际发展动态，具备较强的国际交流与协作能力，能够适应国家经济与社会发展需求，具有创新精神和创业能力的专业人才。
The marine resources and environment focuses on characteristic construction in three directions: marine biotechnology and resource development, environmental pollution monitoring and ecological restoration, and environmental risk assessment. The key is to cultivate students with solid basic theories and knowledge in mathematics, physics, chemistry, and biology, as well as the ability to engage in technology research and management such as investigation and evaluation of marine biological resources and environment, proliferation and conservation of marine biological resources, and sustainable utilization of marine biological resources. They should understand the international development trends of marine biological resources and environment, possess strong international exchange and cooperation abilities, adapt to the needs of national economic and social development, and possess innovative spirit and entrepreneurial ability as professional talents.
三、毕业要求
III．Graduation Requirements
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
基础生态学、海洋生物学、生物化学、环境化学、环境毒理学、生物信息学、生物统计与建模、人体及动物生理学、环境海洋学、微生物学、微流控生物分析技术基础、环境生物修复技术。
Basic Ecology, Marine Biology, Biochemistry, Environmental chemistry, Environmental Toxicology, Bioinformatics, Biostatistics and Modeling, Human and Animal Physiology, Environmental oceanography, Microbiology, Foundation of Microfluidic Technology for Bioanalysis, Environmental bioremediation technology.

毕业要求2 Graduation Requirement 2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂环境工程问题，以获得有效结论。 Problem Analysis: The basic principles of mathematics, natural sciences and engineering sciences can be applied to identify, express, and analyze complex environmental engineering problems through literature research to obtain effective conclusions.	2-1 能够识别和判断复杂环境工程问题的核心特征与关键环节 2-1 to identify and determine the core of complex environmental engineering problems and key links

毕业要求3 Graduation Requirement 3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂环境工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Design / develop solutions: Design solutions for complex environmental engineering problems, design systems, units (components) or processes that meet specific needs, and be able to embody innovation awareness in the design process, taking into account social, health, safety, and law, culture and environment and other factors.	3-1 能够进行复杂工程问题的针对性调研，确定设计目标 3-1 be able to carry out complex engineering problems targeted research to determine the design goals

毕业要求4 Graduation Requirement 4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂环境工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论 Research: It is possible to study complex environmental engineering problems based on scientific principles and scientific methods, including designing experiments, analyzing and interpreting data, and obtaining reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis	4-1 能够基于专业理论，根据对象特征，选择研究路线，设计可行的实验方案，构建实验系统，安全开展实验 4-1 can be based on professional theory, according to the characteristics of the object, select the research route, the design of feasible experimental program, build experimental system, safe to carry out engineering related experiments
毕业要求4 Graduation Requirement 4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂环境工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论 Research: It is possible to study complex environmental engineering problems based on scientific principles and scientific methods, including designing experiments, analyzing and interpreting data, and obtaining reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis	4-2 能够正确采集、整理实验数据，对实验数据和实验结果进行分析与解释，获取合理有效的结论 4-2 can correctly collect and collate the experimental data, analyze and explain the experimental data and experimental results, and obtain reasonable and effective conclusions.
毕业要求5 Graduation Requirement 5 使用现代工具：能够针对复杂环境工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性 The use of modern tools: the ability to develop, select and use appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools for complex environmental engineering issues, including predictions and simulations of complex engineering problems and the ability to understand its limitations	5-1 能够运用环境模拟软件、计算机辅助设计软件等工具，进行复杂环境工程问题的预测、模拟或表达复杂环境工程问题的解决方案，掌握各软件的适用条件 5-1 can use computer-aided design software and other engineering and technical means to predict, simulate or express solutions to complex environmental engineering problems, and master the applicable conditions of software
毕业要求5 Graduation Requirement 5 使用现代工具：能够针对复杂环境工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性 The use of modern tools: the ability to develop, select and use appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools for complex environmental engineering issues, including predictions and simulations of complex engineering problems and the ability to understand its limitations	5-2 能够运用恰当的专业仪器、软件、现代测试方法与技术，进行复杂环境工程问题的数据获取、状态识别及分析研究 5-2 can use appropriate professional instruments, software, modern test methods and techniques for data acquisition, status identification and analysis of complex environmental engineering problems
毕业要求5 Graduation Requirement 5 使用现代工具：能够针对复杂环境工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性 The use of modern tools: the ability to develop, select and use appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools for complex environmental engineering issues, including predictions and simulations of complex engineering problems and the ability to understand its limitations	5-3 具备计算机应用能力，能够运用现代信息平台，获取复杂环境工程问题的相关信息与技术进展 5-3 capable of computer application, able to use modern information platform to obtain relevant information and technical progress of complex environmental engineering problems.
毕业要求6 Graduation Requirement 6 工程与社会：能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任 Engineering and Society: The ability to conduct a rational analysis based on engineering-related background knowledge, evaluate the impact of professional engineering practices and complex engineering problem solutions on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities that should be borne	6-1 能够正确评估环境工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、文化的影响 6-1 can correctly evaluation the impact of environmental engineering practices and complex engineering problem solutions on social, health, safety and culture
毕业要求6 Graduation Requirement 6 工程与社会：能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任 Engineering and Society: The ability to conduct a rational analysis based on engineering-related background knowledge, evaluate the impact of professional engineering practices and complex engineering problem solutions on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities that should be borne	6-2 熟悉复杂环境工程问题的解决中应遵循的法律法规和职业道德规范，明确承担的责任和义务 6-2 familiar with the complex environmental engineering problems should be resolved in accordance with the laws and regulations and professional ethics, clearly assume responsibility and obligations.
毕业要求7 Graduation Requirement 7 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂环境工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响 Environment and Sustainable Development: The ability to understand and evaluate the impact of engineering practices on complex environmental engineering issues on environmental and social sustainable development	7-1 能够正确评价工程实践活动对环境的影响 7-1 can correctly evaluate the engineering practice activities on the environment
毕业要求7 Graduation Requirement 7 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂环境工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响 Environment and Sustainable Development: The ability to understand and evaluate the impact of engineering practices on complex environmental engineering issues on environmental and social sustainable development	7-2 能够在复杂工程问题解决方案中体现对节能和环境友好的要求，树立可持续发展的理念 7-2 to reflect the energy-saving and environment-friendly requirements in the complex engineering problem solution, set up the concept of sustainable development.
毕业要求8 Graduation Requirement 8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任 Professional norms: Have humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility,  understand and comply with engineering ethics and norms in engineering practice, to fulfill responsibilities	8-1 具有正确的人生观、价值观和世界观，具备履行职责的身心条件，维护国家利益，具有推动民族复兴和社会进步的责任感 8-1 have the correct outlook on life, values and world outlook, understand the national conditions, safeguard national interests, with the promotion of national rejuvenation and social progress of the sense of responsibility
毕业要求8 Graduation Requirement 8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任 Professional norms: Have humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility,  understand and comply with engineering ethics and norms in engineering practice, to fulfill responsibilities	8-2 具有人文社会科学素养，理解环境工程伦理的核心理念，在工程实践中自觉遵守职业道德和规范，具有法律意识 8-2 have the humanities and social science literacy, understand the core concept of environmental engineering ethics, consciously abide by professional ethics and norms in engineering practice, with legal awareness.
毕业要求9 Graduation Requirement 9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色 Individuals and Teams: The ability to take on individual, team members, and responsible roles in a multidisciplinary team	9-1 能够独立完成团队分配的工作，具有团队协作意识，具有一定的组织管理能力和较强的自我控制能力、人际交往能力 9-1 be able to independently complete the work of team distribution, have a sense of teamwork, with a certain degree of organizational management and strong self-control, interpersonal skills
毕业要求9 Graduation Requirement 9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色 Individuals and Teams: The ability to take on individual, team members, and responsible roles in a multidisciplinary team	9-2具有跨领域的综合能力，了解与本专业相关学科等领域的技术衔接，具备整合工程应用中所涉及相关学科的综合能力 9-2 the comprehensive ability of cross-field, understand related disciplines and other areas of technical convergence, with the integration of engineering applications involved in the relevant disciplines of comprehensive ability.
毕业要求10 Graduation Requirement 10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流 Communication: The ability to communicate and discuss effectively with industry peers and the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and design submissions, making statements, expressing clearly or responding to directives. And have a certain international perspective, to communicate and discuss in cross-cultural background	10-1 能够通过口头、书面、图表、工程图纸等方式表达思想，与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流 10-1 to express ideas through oral, written, charts, engineering drawings, etc., and communicate and discuss effectively with industry peers and the public
毕业要求10 Graduation Requirement 10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流 Communication: The ability to communicate and discuss effectively with industry peers and the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and design submissions, making statements, expressing clearly or responding to directives. And have a certain international perspective, to communicate and discuss in cross-cultural background	10-2 能够采用一门外国语言，在跨文化背景下进行沟通交流 10-2 be able to use a foreign language to communicate in the context of cross-cultural
毕业要求11 Graduation Requirement 11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用 Project management: To understand and master the principles of project management and economic decision-making methods, and can be applied in a multi-disciplinary environment	11-1 能够对环境工程项目的工艺路线、工艺方案进行技术经济分析、比较和决策 11-1 do technical and economic analysis and have comparison of the technological route and process plan of environmental engineering project
毕业要求11 Graduation Requirement 11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用 Project management: To understand and master the principles of project management and economic decision-making methods, and can be applied in a multi-disciplinary environment	11-2 掌握工程管理原理和工程项目运营的相关管理知识 11-2 master the principles of project management, master the related management knowledge of engineering project operation.
毕业要求12 Graduation Requirement 12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力 Lifelong learning: with independent learning and lifelong learning awareness, have the ability to continue to learn and adapt to development	12-1 具有自主学习和终身学习意识，具备终身学习的知识基础，掌握自主学习的方法，了解拓展知识和能力的途径 12-1  with independent learning and lifelong learning awareness, with a lifelong learning knowledge base, master the way of self-learning, understanding of ways to expand knowledge and ability
毕业要求12 Graduation Requirement 12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力 Lifelong learning: with independent learning and lifelong learning awareness, have the ability to continue to learn and adapt to development	12-2 能针对个人或职业发展需求，采用合适的方法，自主学习，适应环境工程领域的发展 12-2 for personal or career development needs, to use appropriate methods to go on self-learning and adapt to the development of environmental engineering field.

1.全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程 ，需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 毕业要求1 Graduation requirement I 理论基础知识：具备将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识应用于海洋科学领域复杂科学问题的能力。 Theoretical basic knowledge: the ability to apply mathematics, natural sciences, engineering fundamentals and expertise to complex issues in the field of Marine Science.	1-1 能够将高等数学、线性代数、概率论与数理统计等数学知识综合运用到复杂海洋科学问题的表述和解决之中； 1-1 Apply advanced mathematics, linear algebra, probability theory and mathematical statistics and other mathematical knowledge to the complex representation and solution of marine science problems;
毕业要求1 Graduation requirement I 理论基础知识：具备将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识应用于海洋科学领域复杂科学问题的能力。 Theoretical basic knowledge: the ability to apply mathematics, natural sciences, engineering fundamentals and expertise to complex issues in the field of Marine Science.	1-2能够运用物理、化学及生物学等相关知识理解并掌握海洋调查、海洋环境监测、海洋污染治理与生态修复、海洋环境管理与规划的基本原理和技术方法； 1-2 Understand and master the basic principles of marine technology applying physics, chemistry, biology and other related knowledge in Marine pollution monitoring, Vessel-source pollution control and ecological restoration, Marine environment management and planning;
毕业要求1 Graduation requirement I 理论基础知识：具备将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识应用于海洋科学领域复杂科学问题的能力。 Theoretical basic knowledge: the ability to apply mathematics, natural sciences, engineering fundamentals and expertise to complex issues in the field of Marine Science.	1-3 掌握物理海洋学、化学海洋学、海洋地质学、海洋生物学、海洋遥感技术等基础知识，并能应用于解决实际海洋科学问题。 1-3 Master the basic knowledge of physical oceanography, chemical oceanography, marine geology, marine biology, and marine remote sensing technology, and apply to solve the practical problems of marine science.
毕业要求2 Graduation requirement II 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂海洋科学问题，以获得有效结论。 Problem Analysis: The basic principles of mathematics, natural sciences and engineering sciences can be applied to identify, express, and analyze complex Marine Science problems through literature research to obtain effective conclusions.	2-1 针对实际问题选择恰当的数学、物理、化学等相关知识进行推理分析； 2-1 Select the appropriate mathematics, physics, chemistry and other related knowledge to reasoning and analysis in view of the practical problems;
毕业要求2 Graduation requirement II 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂海洋科学问题，以获得有效结论。 Problem Analysis: The basic principles of mathematics, natural sciences and engineering sciences can be applied to identify, express, and analyze complex Marine Science problems through literature research to obtain effective conclusions.	2-2在充分理解和掌握专业知识的基础上，能够运用所学知识开展文献检索和资料查询，并依据所获得的知识进行合理的问题分析，以获得有效结论。 2-2 On the basis of full understanding and mastering of professional knowledge, carry out the literature search and data query utilizing learned knowledge, and make reasonable problem analysis in order to obtain the effective conclusions based on the knowledge obtained.
毕业要求3 Graduation requirement III 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂海洋科学问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 Research: It is possible to study complex Marine Science problems based on scientific principles and scientific methods, including designing experiments, analyzing and interpreting data, and obtaining reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis.	3-1 结合海洋科学专业基本原理和专业基础知识，设计科学实验进行探索和分析讨论，并优化实验技术与工程方案； 3-1 Based on the basic principles and professional knowledge of marine science, design scientific experiments for exploratory, analysis and discussion, and optimize the experimental technology and engineering program；
毕业要求3 Graduation requirement III 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂海洋科学问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 Research: It is possible to study complex Marine Science problems based on scientific principles and scientific methods, including designing experiments, analyzing and interpreting data, and obtaining reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis.	3-2 综合运用海洋科学专业知识开展研究性实验，并得到合理有效的结论。 3-2 Carry out research experiments with comprehensive utilization of professional knowledge of Marine Science, and get a reasonable effective conclusion.
毕业要求4 Graduation requirement IV 使用现代工具：能够针对复杂海洋科学问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 The use of modern tools: the ability to develop, select and use appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools for complex Marine Science issues, including predictions and simulations of complex engineering problems and the ability to understand its limitations.	4-1 理解并掌握获取相关信息的必要性与基本方法，能够运用图书馆资源进行文献检索和资料查询； 4-1 Understand and grasp the necessity and basic methods of obtaining relevant information, and use the library resources to carry out the literature search and data query；
毕业要求4 Graduation requirement IV 使用现代工具：能够针对复杂海洋科学问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 The use of modern tools: the ability to develop, select and use appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools for complex Marine Science issues, including predictions and simulations of complex engineering problems and the ability to understand its limitations.	4-2 掌握开发、选择、使用恰当的技术和资源，运用现代科技工具和信息技术以解决实际复杂的海洋调查和海洋环境监测中遇到问题的能力。 4-2 Master appropriate technologies and resources about development, selection and utilization, use modern science technology tools and information technology to obtain professional knowledge for solving complex engineering problems.
毕业要求5 Graduation requirement V 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在实践中理解并遵守职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Professional norms: Have humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility, understand and comply with ethics and norms in practice, to fulfill responsibilities.	5-1 能够不断地提高自身的人文社会科学素养； 5-1 Continuously improve the quality of Humanities and Social Sciences literacy;
毕业要求5 Graduation requirement V 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在实践中理解并遵守职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Professional norms: Have humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility, understand and comply with ethics and norms in practice, to fulfill responsibilities.	5-2 具备科学的世界观、人生观和价值观； 5-2 Possess the scientific world outlook, outlook on life and values;
毕业要求5 Graduation requirement V 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在实践中理解并遵守职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Professional norms: Have humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility, understand and comply with ethics and norms in practice, to fulfill responsibilities.	5-3 具备责任心和社会责任感，懂法守法； 5-3 Have a sense of conscientiousness and social responsibility, observe disciplines and obey laws;
毕业要求5 Graduation requirement V 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在实践中理解并遵守职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Professional norms: Have humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility, understand and comply with ethics and norms in practice, to fulfill responsibilities.	5-4 注重职业道德修养，用人单位评价好并具有一定社会反响。 5-4 Emphasize occupation morality, employer evaluation and certain social repercussions.
毕业要求6 Graduation requirement VI 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Individuals and Teams: The ability to take on individual, team members, and responsible roles in a multidisciplinary team.	6-1 能够理解团队合作的意义，能与团队成员有效沟通，用人单位和社会评价好； 6-1 Understand the meaning of teamwork, communicate effectively with team members and employers with favorable social evaluation;
毕业要求6 Graduation requirement VI 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Individuals and Teams: The ability to take on individual, team members, and responsible roles in a multidisciplinary team.	6-2 能在团队中根据角色要求发挥应起的作用，工作能力得到充分体现。 6-2 Play an important role in a team based on role requirements, fully embody your working abilities.
毕业要求7 Graduation requirement VII 沟通：能够就复杂问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。Communication: The ability to communicate and discuss effectively with industry peers and the public on complex issues, including writing reports and design submissions, making statements, expressing clearly or responding to directives. And have a certain international perspective, to communicate and discuss in cross-cultural background.	7-1 能够通过口头或书面方式表达自己的想法，就复杂科学问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流； 7-1 Express your ideas through oral or written form, communicate and exchange effectively with the industry peers and the public for complex scientific problems;
毕业要求7 Graduation requirement VII 沟通：能够就复杂问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。Communication: The ability to communicate and discuss effectively with industry peers and the public on complex issues, including writing reports and design submissions, making statements, expressing clearly or responding to directives. And have a certain international perspective, to communicate and discuss in cross-cultural background.	7-2 至少掌握一门外语，对海洋科学专业及其相关领域的国内外状况有基本的了解，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 7-2 Master a foreign language at least, have basic understanding of the domestic and international status of marine science and related fields, communicate and exchange with others under the cross cultural background.
毕业要求8 Graduation requirement VIII 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。Lifelong learning: with independent learning and lifelong learning awareness, have the ability to continue to learn and adapt to development.	8-1 对于自我探索和学习的必要性有正确的认识； 8-1 Have a correct understanding of the necessity of self-exploration and learning;
毕业要求8 Graduation requirement VIII 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。Lifelong learning: with independent learning and lifelong learning awareness, have the ability to continue to learn and adapt to development.	8-2 能够采取适合的方式通过学习发展自身能力，并表现出自我学习和探索的成效。 8-2 Develop own abilities adopting appropriate ways through learning, and show the effectiveness of self-learning and exploration.

1.全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程 ，需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. For details, please refer to the regulations on student status management in the student handbook.	1.全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程 ，需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. [Table 7]
毕业要求1 Requirement  I	专业基础知识：具有坚实的环境学、海洋学和生物学的基本理论和专业知识，掌握海洋环境毒理学监测与评价、海洋生物技术与资源开发等技能，具有从事海洋污染调查、环境毒理学检测和评价、海洋生态修复及海洋生物资源开发的基本能力。 Professional knowledge: Having a solid basic theories and professional knowledge of environmental science, oceanography and biology; mastering the skills of marine environmental toxicology monitoring and evaluation, marine biotechnology and resource development; havingthe basic ability to engage in marine pollution investigation, environmental toxicology testing and evaluation, as well as marine ecological restoration and marine biological resource development.
毕业要求2 Requirement II	工具学科基础知识：能够掌握数学、生物信息学、生物统计建模等基础理论和方法解决环境、健康和生态问题。 Basic knowledge of Tool subjects: Be able to master basic theories and methods such as mathematics, bioinformatics, and biostatistical modeling to solve environmental, health and ecological problems.
毕业要求3 Requirement III	问题分析及科学研究能力：能够应用后基因组时代的大数据获取和监测技术，通过文献调研，识别、表达并提出分析问题解决问题的方案，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 Problem analysis and scientific research capacity: Ability to apply the big data acquisition and monitoring technology in the post-genome era, identify, express and propose solutions to analyze problems through literature research, including designing experiments, analyzing and interpreting data, and drawing reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis.
毕业要求4 Requirement IV	使用现代工具的能力：能够针对专业领域，使用环境监测和系统生物学分析手段，完成数据的获取、分析和结果分析。 The ability to use modern tools: Capable of data acquisition, analysis and results analysis using environmental monitoring and systems biology analysis for specialized fields.
毕业要求5 Requirement V	职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在环境与生态和健康等领域实践中理解并遵守职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Professional norms: Possess humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility, and be able to understand and comply with professional ethics and norms in the field of environment, ecology and health, to fulfill their responsibilities.
毕业要求6 Requirement VI	个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Individuals and Teams: Ability to work as an individual, a team member and a leader in a multidisciplinary team.
毕业要求7 Requirement VII	沟通能力：能够就复杂环境问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 Communication: ability to communicate with industry peers and the public on complex environmental issues effectively, including writing reports and designing manuscripts, presenting statements, expressing clearly or responding to directives. And have a certain international perspective, to communicate and exchange in the cross-cultural background.
毕业要求8 Requirement VIII	终身学习的能力：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 Lifelong learning ability: having independent learning and lifelong learning awareness, having the ability to continue learning and adapt to development.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. For details, please refer to the regulations on student status management in the student handbook.	1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits.
